
1.1(1): gsang chen mthar thug ma rgyud thugs rje nyi ma 
1.2(1): gzhi ye sangs rgyas pa'i rgyud 
1.3(1): bzhugs so/ /
1.4(1): @#/ /zhang zhung skad du/ u ye tha tson ma tra she rkya nyi ri ku shu ha sangs kyin tan 
1.5(1): tra/ bod skad du/ gsang chen mthar thug ma rgyud thugs rje nyi ma gzhi' ye sangs 
1.6(1): rgyas pa'i rgyud/ ston pa kun tu bzang po mkha' 'gying dkar po/ gsang ba gsang 
1.7(1): chen gsang mchog mthar thug la phyag 'tshal lo/ /
1.8(1): 7 'di skad bdag gis thos pa'i dus gcig na/ bon nyid mi 'gyur ba g.yung 
1.9(1): drung gi dbyings/ ye shes 'od du gsal ba'i mkha'/ dus gsum nub pa med pa'i 
1.10(1): klong / 'og min 'da' ba med pa'i pho brang / 'gyur med g.yung drung gtam pa'i brag 
1.11(1): steng / theg chen 'khor lo bskor ba'i zhing khams/ bde ldan pad ma rgyas pa'i gdan 
1.12(1): thog /bsam 'phel rin chen bdal ba'i dkyil 'khor/ ye shes me ri 'bar ba'i klong 
1.13(1): gur na/ ston pa kun tu bzang po gsang mchog rgyal po de/ sku snang la rang bzhin 
1.14(1): med par zhal phyogs bcu yongs la gzigs pa/ gsung brjod bya las 'das par 
1.15(1): ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo nas bon ston pa/ thugs dgongs dus gsum sangs rgyas thams 
1.16(1): cad kyi mkhyen yul gsal ba/ yon tan dang phrin las thams cad brtsal ba med 
2.1(1): par lhun gyis grub pa de/ 'khor phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas rnams dang / rigs lnga'i 
2.2(1): bder gshegs rnams dang / sa bcu'i g.yung drung sems dpa' rnams dang / ru 
2.3(1): bzhi'i dbal tshogs rnams dang / zhing lnga'i mkha' 'gro rnams dang / lha 'khor dang 
2.4(1): gsas 'khor bsam du med pa la/ bdud rtsi'i chu bo yi rgyun bzhin bon ston no/ /

2.6(1): ba la pha rgyud lung chen nam mkha' lta bur bstan no//bsgom pa la dga' ba la don 
2.7(1): rgyud theg chen nor bu lta bur bstan no//spyod pa la dga' ba la dbal lung rgyud 
2.8(1): chen rgya mtsho lta bu bstan no/ /'bras bu la dga' ba la sgom rgyud rdzogs chen nyi ma 
2.9(1): lta bur bstan no/ /bsgrub pa la dga' ba la sngags rgyud gsas mkhar chen po u 
2.10(1): du 'bar ba lta bur bstan pa la/ de'i nang nas yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs 
2.11(1): rgyas myur du thob par byed pa'i lam la mngon par spyod pa'i snang bar/ ston pas 
2.12(1): zhal bdun nas dus gcig gsungs par rtogs so/ /dung 'od 'bar ba'i zhal 
2.13(1): nas/ 'phrul gshen snang ldan la sogs gshen rab brgyad khri bzhi stong la/ gsang 
2.14(1): mchog gsang ba'i dbyings grol bla na med pa'i rgyud gsungs so/ /g.yu 'od 'bar 
2.15(1): ba'i zhal nas/ 'chi med gtsug phud las sogs ye gshen sum brgya drug bcu la/
2.16(1): che mchog dbal gsas rngam pa sku'i rgyud gsungs so/ /gser 'od 'bar ba'i zhal 
2.17(1): nas/ gsang ba 'dus pa las sogs lha bon brgya bcu la/ gtso' mchog mkha' 
2.18(1): 'gying thugs kyi rgyud gsungs so/ /mthing nag 'bar ba'i zhal nas/ stag la me 
2.19(1): 'bar las sogs dbal bon drug cu la khro mchog 'brug gsas chem pa phrin las 
2.20(1): kyi rgyud gsungs so/ /zangs 'od 'bar ba'i zhal nas/ bzang za ring btsun las

4.1(1): pas go cha brtsan/ smin grol dngos su grub pas bde chen mchog (myong ) /mchog 
4.2(1): 'bras dbyings grub sad stor 'byams 'phrang bsgral/ don 'bras dbyings grub

4.10(1): shes g.yung drung ston/ skye med thig le ye shes dbyings la rdzogs/ ston pa'i thig le 
4.11(1): ye shes kun bzang 'od/ lung gi thig le ye shes kun 'byung gsal/ rgyud kyi thig le 
4.12(1): rig pa thabs chen mchog /man ngag thig le yang dag nges par gsal/ lta ba'i 
4.13(1): thig le rtogs pa'i rding du gyur/ spyod pa'i thig le ma chags rnam par dag /phrin 
4.14(1): las thig le brtsal med lhun gyis grub/ lam gyi thig le ye shes bgrod du med/
4.15(1): dgongs pa'i thig le ye shes mi g.yo gsal/ ting 'dzin thig le ye shes mi 'gyur 
4.16(1): gsal/ thugs rje'i thig le ye shes kun la snyoms/ shes rab thig le mtshan ma'i

4.20(1): kyi thig le dmigs med de bzhin gsal/ gsal ba'i thig le mtshon pa yongs dang

10.20(1): can/ lus kyi mthar thug rtogs pa'i ye shes sku/ sgom pa'i stobs kyis gsal la 
10.21(1): tshad mar byed/ rjes dpag tshad mas mdzod la rnam dpyod na/ zhugs 'jug ldog 
11.1(1): pa'i shes rab dag pas rtogs/ zhugs pa yul la phyogs cig bon du bzung /
11.2(1): 'jug pa dpe la gom pas rjes su nges/ ldog pa mi mthun phyogs la med par mkhyen/
11.3(1): de skyon 'khrul pa'i yid dang rtog pa'i sems/ shes bya gshis dang shes pa rang la 
11.4(1): yod/ rtog pa 'khrul pa'i blo ni spyi skyon te/ dbang po gshis 'khrul gzhan gyi rnam 
11.5(1): par 'tshe/ rang 'khrul mthong ba'i bag chags 'khrul pa'i blo/ yid kyi gshis 'khrul 
11.6(1): 'khor ba'i gdung ba ste/ rang 'khrul yid kyi bslu ba 'khrul pa'i blo/ rang rig gshis 
11.7(1): 'khrul rmi lam sgyu ma ste/ rang 'khrul las kyi rkyen dos 'khrul pa'i blo/ sems nyid 
11.8(1): gshis 'khrul mtshan mar 'dzin pa ste/ rang 'khrul rgyun gyi g.yeng ba 'khrul pa'i blo/
11.9(1): rtog 'khrul de dgu spangs pas dbyings dgu rtogs/sgo bzhi bon gyi sgros 'dogs 
11.10(1): chod pa yin/ mngon rjes gzhan bzhi dgos nus 'dir chung yang / zab dkar 
11.11(1): grub mtha' rang rig med thabs med/ ye shes gzhi ma rang rig bu gnyis ni/ rgyang 
11.12(1): ring skyo ngas ma mjal stor ba la/ ma pang bu rgyug 'dres pa'i yon tan gsum/
11.13(1): g.yang zas mi tshugs ma yi bu skyong 'dra/ rig pas ma 'khyams bus khug bon nyid 
11.14(1): zin/ rang rig ngo shes bu stor rgyal sras rnyed/ mngon gsum tshad ma'i yon tan 
11.15(1): don cher 'gyur/ bskyed na bskyed byed rang rig sangs rgyas 'byung / rtogs na 
11.16(1): rtogs myong rang rig ye shes 'thob/ 'khrul na 'khrul myong rang rig rang ngo shes/
11.17(1): ngos bzung 'di ni skad cig sangs rgyas mchog /shes pa nyid kyi don chen dam pa 
11.18(1): 'grub/ grub mtha'i gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ rtsa ba zab dkar rgya mtsho nyag 
11.19(1): mar sbas/ ma rig rig pa'i sangs rgyas thob mchog yin/ tshad mas lta sa lta byed 
11.20(1): man ngag 'di/ grub mtha' gzhan lugs bshad pas spros pa chod/ lta thabs tshad 
11.21(1): mar bstan pas sgro 'dogs med/ rtog 'khrul blo rkyen bsal bas 'khrul gzhi med/
12.1(1): gzigs tshad thad kam sbyar bas go mi nor/ ye shes tsir bzung byas pas rang rig 
12.2(1): rnyed/ mchog chen mchog gi grub mtha' gsang mchog yin/ 'khrul sgrib gol gsum 
12.3(1): gzhi skyon bsal byas nas/ yin snang shar gsum gsang chen gsang ba'i lung /
12.4(1): yin pa rang byung ye shes bon sku yin/ snang ba rang snang ye shes rdzogs skur snang /
12.5(1): shar ba rang rig ye shes sprul skur shar/ log dman 'khyar gsum lam skyon ma gos 
12.6(1): pa'i/ zab myur mtho gsum thugs rje nyi ma'i lam/ zab pa ma rgyud gsang sngags 
12.7(1): gdam pa'i mchog /myur ba a dkar theg pa chen po'i rtse/ mtho ba bsgrod pa kun gyi 
12.8(1): lam phugs yin/ sad stor 'byams gsum 'bras skyon yongs grol ba/ gsang 
12.9(1): mchog mthar thug 'bras bu bla na med/ gsang ba'i bon rnams kun gyi nying khu 
12.10(1): 'dus/ mchog gi ye sangs rgyas pa'i ngo bo thob/ mthar thug bla med 'dren pa zad 
12.11(1): kyi rtse/ zhes bka' bstsal to/ /gzhi ye sangs rgyas par bshad pa/ gsang chen ma 
12.12(1): rgyud/ kun gzhi ye shes lhun grub kyi le'u ste gnyis pa'o// //
12.13(1): 7 kye ma 'od mtsho yum gyis yang zhus pa/ snang gzhi sku gsum lhun grub ci ltar 
12.14(1): lags/ snang srid thig le bdag la bshad du gsol/ de la kun tu bzang pos 
12.15(1): bka' stsal pa/
12.16(1): 7 snang srid thig le ye shes mkha' la shar/ snang srid sprul dang cig bsdus 
12.17(1): gsal bar gnas/ mkha' lnga'i 'byor 'brel shar dus bstan pa'o/ /ci ltar 'char 
12.18(1): lugs rnam pa lngas 'chad de/ dang po rang byung ye shes chen po'i rtsal/ dag pa'i 
12.19(1): sku dang zhing khams bsam mtha' yas/ ma dag thugs rje'i thabs kyis 'dul ba la/
12.20(1): snang ba phyi dang srid pa nang sprul ste/ ma g.yos dbyings chen ye shes lhun gyis grub/
12.21(1): snod bcud thugs rjes bzung bar mdzad pa'i phyir/ dbyings las dbyings bstan 
13.1(1): nam mkha' yangs dog med/ de las ye shes gsal ba'i sa bon du/ dkar ser 
13.2(1): dmar ljang thon kha 'bar ba'i 'od/ rdzu 'phrul rlung gis bskyod cing bskor ba las/
13.3(1): nam mkha' rlung me chu dang sa rnams grub/ ri rab gling bzhi gling phran dpag bsam 
13.4(1): dang / stong gsum stong gi 'jig rten thams cad 'byung / 'byung ba lnga yi dwangs ma 
13.5(1): bcud 'dus pa/ 'od sgra nyi zla rin chen go 'byed rgyan/ 'di ltar snang ba sgyu ma'i 
13.6(1): kun rdzob shar/ rang byung rig pa ye shes dri med de/ srid pa nang la 'byung 'jug 
13.7(1): rnam pa gsum/ dag pa dag bdo' ma dag rim pa bzhin/ spyi gtsug mgo dang lus 
13.8(1): la zhugs pa'i tshe/ yi ge'i rnam pa a dkar ha dmar po/ 'gro drug las kyi sa bon 
13.9(1): rim pa bzhin/ skye sgo bzhi yi rten la bab ma thag /lhan skyes lhas sleb 'od kyi rten 
13.10(1): la bsten/ mnyam 'ong bdud byung las kyi rlung gis g.yos/ 'thab pa'i stobs kyis 
13.11(1): 'od las zer du 'phros/ sems las yid sprul kun bzang yab yum gnyis/ pha 
13.12(1): ma'i sta la babs nas las kyi 'phrad/ dga' bde tshad med ye shes gcig du 'dres/
13.13(1): sems kyi rten gyur rang mdangs dag pa'i 'od/ dkar ljang dmar ba'i rang bzhin 
13.14(1): dri med dang / ci la mi rtog stong gsal bde ba'i sku/ rig pa'i ye shes tshon gang 
13.15(1): 'od la gnas/ bon sku thig le nyag gcig kun bzang de/ 'khor ba'i gnas na 
13.16(1): bzhugs kyang bon nyid dbyings/ bde chen ngang la mi g.yo rnam rtog med/ dbyings 
13.17(1): kyi rang byung ye shes chen po dang / don gyi rang rig ye shes dri med 'dres/ dus 
13.18(1): gsum dus med ka dag mngon du gyur/ thig le nyag gcig g.yung drung sku mnga' 
13.19(1): ba/ bon sku bde' chen ngang la zhag gcig bzhugs/ brten gnas 'og min 'da' 
13.20(1): ba med pa'i gnas/ dkar la khod snyoms dri med lha yi yul/ blo skyon med pa'i 
13.21(1): gtsang la nyams dga' rtogs/ ye shes rang 'od rin chen gur lngar mthong / rnam 
14.1(1): rtog bral bas yangs zhing rgya chen po/ las kyi rlung ni rtsal chen seng ge'i khri/ mngal 
14.2(1): gyi drod rlung dri med pad ma'i gdan/ thig le dkar dmar thabs shes nyi zla'i steng /
14.3(1): lhan skyes bdud ni rang grol chen po'i gdan/ rang rig ye shes gsang mchog rdzogs 
14.4(1): pa'i sku/ ye shes ting 'dzin rang lus mtshan dper 'char/ shes bya'i yon tan rin 
14.5(1): chen mdzes dgu'i brgyan/ 'dus byas dge tshogs lha yi na bza'i mdangs/ lhan 
14.6(1): skyes lha ni gnyis med bde ba'i yum/ pho mo ma ning byang sems dkar dmar 
14.7(1): brten/ gsal ba'i tshad ni 'od gsal lha dang 'dra/ bde ba rab rgyas dang po'i 
14.8(1): sa thob bzhin/ mi rtog stong pa'i ngang la dga' dgu spyod/ dkar gsal sku dang 
14.9(1): dmar 'bar sgeg pa mo/ /mthing 'brang gzi brjid chen po'i lus po can/ g.yas 
14.10(1): g.yon dbus mthing rtsa gsum skye ba yi/ 'od la brten nas rgyal ba longs spyod 
14.11(1): rdzogs/ mtshan dpe' ldan pa'i sku ru zhag gcig bzhugs/ de nas zhag re bzhin 
14.12(1): du rang rig gi/ ye shes gnas 'gyur stong nyid mnyam nyid dang / bya nan me long 
14.13(1): so sor rtogs par 'gyur/ bde chen longs spyod bon dang sprul pa dang / thabs 
14.14(1): shes 'khor lo rim par bab pa'i ltas/ rin chen sna lnga'i khang bzang nyams dga' 
14.15(1): 'bar/ so so'i zhing khams grangs bcas dkyil 'khor dbus/ rigs rtags lta 
14.16(1): bu'i gdan mchog dam pa der/ rab la sprul pa'i sku mchog 'dul ba drug /dad 
14.17(1): ldan 'khor la bon gyi longs spyod ston/ 'bring la rigs drug dbang po brgya byin 
14.18(1): ltar/ snang srid dkor dang rgyal po'i snang ba 'char/ mthar yang rang lus gang 
14.19(1): len 'bangs su mthong / bran khol zas noRa 'jig rten snang ba 'char/ lha'i gnas 
14.20(1): dang lha min mi yul gling / byol song sde chen yi dwags la sogs pa/ las kyi 'brel 
14.21(1): tshad lhag par gsal bar mkhyen/ ye shes gcig la kun bzang mkhyen gzigs 
15.1(1): gnyis/ gsal stong bde gsum ye shes lngar bstan kyang / ye shes thig le bzhi bcu 
15.2(1): rtsa lnga de/ phan chad dus der tshang ba'i sangs rgyas 'dra/ bde chen 'khor lo lnga la 
15.3(1): brten byas nas/ gang la gang 'dul 'gro ba'i rim pa bzhin/ cir yang sprul pa'i 
15.4(1): sku ru zhag lnga bzhugs/ ye shes de la lus su sprul pa'i tshul/ bdun phrag gnyis par 
15.5(1): rang rig bsngang zhing 'phro/ gsum par mngal gyis dbang byas myos pa ste/ bzhi par 
15.6(1): lhan skyes lhas dbang lhag par gsal/ lnga par mnyam 'ong bdud dbang 'thib par 
15.7(1): byed/ bdun phrag lnga rdzogs zla gcig zhag lnga la/ ye shes thig le cha bzhi 'grib par 
15.8(1): 'gyur/ de nas bdun phrag bco lnga rim pa bzhin/ srid pa'i lha lnga 'byung ba'i lha lnga 
15.9(1): dang / bskal pa'i lha lngas dbang byas zla lnga'i bar/ nyi shu phyed dang gnyis kyi ye shes 
15.10(1): 'grib/ dbang po ma chags bar der nyi shu dang / phyed bzhi ye shes yod pas mkhyen 
15.11(1): spyod 'bring / de nas zla bzhi ngo lnga'i bar phan chad/ pho la so lnga mo la so gnyis kyis/
15.12(1): bdun phrag re bzhin ye shes cha re 'grib/ de nas skye 'gyur ye shes bcu lus chung /
15.13(1): zla gcig sems nyid dngos dbang phyed lnga 'grib/ zla gnyis rang rig dbang bar 
15.14(1): phyed gsum 'das/ zla gsum yid yod ye shes gnyis lus sdud/ zla bzhi dbang po 
15.15(1): yod nas gzhi la nub/ de yi bar la rtsa rgyas lus rgyas pas/ rang byung ye shes je 
15.16(1): che 'grib pa ste/ lus bskyed shed rdzogs dug lnga'i klong du nub/ zla dgu ngo bcu skyes 
15.17(1): nas zla gsum bar/ ye shes zhe lnga de ltar rdzogs tshul ston/ de dus ye shes thig le 
15.18(1): ci ltar na/ ye shes nub dang 'gag pa don la med/ kun rdzob rang snang dbang gis 
15.19(1): 'grib na yang / ye shes mthu las dbus mthing bsam gtan rtsa/ yar sne tshang bug 
15.20(1): mar sne gsang bar zug / sangs rgyas gyen 'phags sems dpa' brjes pa'i tshul/
15.21(1): ring thung tshe las phra sbom bsod nams ste/ yangs dog ye shes drang 'khyog bzang 
16.1(1): ngan ston/ g.yas dkar g.yon dmar dbus la 'khril nas yod/ mar sne lte 'og 
16.2(1): yar sne sna sgor dod/ de las gyes pas 'khor lo lnga po ni/ spyi bo bde chen rtsa 'dab 
16.3(1): so gnyis pa/ ye shes bzhi sbyor dbang ba'i 'khor lo yin/ mgrin pa longs spyod rtsa 
16.4(1): 'dab bcu drug pa/ ye shes tshogs brgyad dbang ba'i 'khor lo yin/ thugs ka bon 
16.5(1): nyid rtsa 'dab bcu gnyis pa/ ye shes rigs bzhi dbang ba'i 'khor lo yin/ lte ba

16.7(1): gsang ba thabs shes 'khor lo rtsa 'dab bcu/ ye shes rnam brgyad dbang ba'i 'khor

16.9(1): phyi rtsa khrag rgyu nang rtsa sbags mar rgyu/ gsang rtsa rlung rgyu rtsa chen brgya rtsa brgyad/ rtsa 
16.10(1): bran sum brgya brgyad khri bzhi stong gyes/ g.yog nas ye shes rtsa rnams zum pa yi/
16.11(1): mkhyen spyod rdzu 'phrul sbas pa'i tshul du gnas/ ye shes lus la gnas pa'i tshul 
16.12(1): bstan pa/ ma dag 'byung lnga dag pa 'od lnga yang / yang dag ye shes lnga yis 'gro 
16.13(1): don byed/ mkha' yi lha mos stong nyid nam mkha' sprul/ thams cad gsal ba'i go 
16.14(1): rnams phye ba'o/ /rlung gi lha mos mnyam nyid dbugs su sprul/ brtan shing 'degs 
16.15(1): byed thams cad yongs su bus/ me yi lha mos sor rtogs drod du sprul/ gsal 
16.16(1): bar mdangs 'byin thams cad smin par byas/ chu yi lha mos me long rlan du sprul/
16.17(1): gsher zhing rlabs sdud rlan byed chu yis gso'/ sa yi lha mos nan tan sha ru sprul/
16.18(1): sra mkhregs brten pa'i stobs kyis yongs su bskyed/ ye shes gnas kyang bag nyal

17.1(1): bzhin nam mkha' 'od dkar mig snying ngo /mkha' ni snying rten mig dod gsang 
17.2(1): mchog gnas/ rlung gi glo rten snar dod khu byug gnas/ me ni mchin rten lcer dod 
17.3(1): ye shes gnas/ chu ni mkhal rten rnar dod rgyal po gnas/ sa ni mtsher rten ba 
17.4(1): spu g.yung drung ngo / /lha rnams gnas na tsha grang 'du ba'i nad/ yod par mi rig 
17.5(1): med na gnas pa 'gal/ma gsal gsal dang mngon rdzogs rim pas sbyor/ ye 
17.6(1): shes gnas na mkhyen spyod rtsal stobs dgos/ mi dmigs phyir na shar ba gang zhe 
17.7(1): na/ 'char ba'i dus la rnam pa gsum yod de/ skyes dus lhan skyes ye shes nyams su 
17.8(1): myong / de dus 'char tshul gong du gsal bar bstan/ 'chi dus bon nyid 'od 
17.9(1): gsal ma bu mjal/ de tshe 'char ba 'og nas bar dor ston/ tshe 'dir 'char ba

17.11(1): mkhyen dang mngon shes rdzu 'phrul dang / rang lus sprul bsgyur 'bum phrag nges med 
17.12(1): pa/ mkha' la lding dang chu la bying ba med/ dga' ldan 'gro dang sa 'og gter 
17.13(1): rnams 'byin/ mi min bon nyan thugs dam zhal gzigs sogs/ mchog dang thun 
17.14(1): mong ting 'dzin zas za dang / bsam gyis mi khyab ye shes rtsal las 'char/ zhes

18.1(1): pa gzugs ste sku bzhi snang bar shar/ de phyir gting 'chol rim skye rtsad mi chod/
18.2(1): gzhan tshol (gzha' tshon ) dor nas lhag pa'i bden mthong ba/
18.3(1): 7 bon nyid thig le ye shes dbyings la rdzogs/ bon nyid ngos 'dzin skur bstan 
18.4(1): ye shes gnas/ dbyings las spyod dang rdzogs pa'i zhing khams bstan/ de yang 
18.5(1): mkha' la sprin char myu gu bzhin/ med las yod 'byung rang byung ye shes de/ yin pa 
18.6(1): don gyi ngos nas ngo bo gcig /bzhi bcu lnga dang brgyad khri nyag gcig ma/ snang ba 
18.7(1): yon tan ngos nas khyad par che/ gcig las brgyad khri grangs med 'gro la snang /

18.10(1): gzhi/ de la sku med stong pa mu bzhi 'dra/ nag po kha 'byams las 'das bon nyid sku/
18.11(1): rang mdangs ye shes 'od gsal mkhyen rab can/ mdun rgyab mi mnga' thugs rje'i 
18.12(1): 'od zer 'phro/ sku la ye shes med na rig med dam/ dngos po ther zug sangs rgyas 
18.13(1): ma yin pas/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i rgyal po ye rig bcas/ 'khrul med mi 'gyur 
18.14(1): rtog med cir yang gsal/ bdag med sangs rgyas 'chi med lhun gyis grub/ ye 
18.15(1): shes dbyings la mi spyod bya long 'dra/ rang sangs rgyas kyang ma khong bu shi bzhin/
18.16(1): des na rang rig rgya yan thogs med 'phyo/ mu med 'byams yas rgya ma chad pa'i 
18.17(1): dbyings/ gar yang khyab cing dgos 'byung rgya cher gnas/ dbyings las rdzogs pa'i 
18.18(1): mthu med chad lta 'dra/ stong lha (lta)stong ste mun nag gling dgu bzhin/ des na yon 
18.19(1): tan gsung thugs sku phrin las/ gsas mkhar chen po mchog lnga'i zhing khams rdzogs/
18.20(1): khyad par thugs rje nyi ma 'bum shar dang / stong shar bzhi shar brgya dang drug bcu 
18.21(1): sogs/ bsdus pas rang byung yang dag mthar thug sku/ gzhi las rtsal shar bcu 
19.1(1): gnyis tshan lnga las/ dkyil 'khor rtsa ba'i lha tshogs drug bcur 'gyur/ lam drug 
19.2(1): zhing skyong mngon spyod gnas srung dang /ltang 'dzin tshad por brgya dang don bzhi'o/ /

19.4(1): 'bras bu mngon 'gyur gsang mchog yab yum brgyad/ 'bras bu don byed tshad med

19.6(1): lnga'i lha/ phyi nang gsang ba'i zhing khams gnas lugs bstan/ rang bzhin bon nyid 
19.7(1): dbyings nas lhun grub pa'i/ mkha' 'dra gzhal med khang chen 'byams yas pa/
19.8(1): bsod nams ye shes tshogs las grub pa yi/ bsam gyis mi khyab dpag med zhing 
19.9(1): khams lnga/ 'jig rten 'jig tshogs 'das pa'i khyams khang gnyis/ tshogs sbyor

19.11(1): can/ thabs shes dbyings shes sku lnga bla med tog /sangs rgyas ye shes sangs rgyas 
19.12(1): thugs rje stobs/ brjod kyis mi lang bsam pa'i tshad la 'das/ mkha' la sprin chen 
19.13(1): 'khrigs pa'i mthu med na/ sa la lo 'bras 'khrung par mi 'gyur bzhin/ dbyings kyi 
19.14(1): zhing khams nus pa'i stobs rtsal las/ 'jig rten rten dang brten med dkyil

19.18(1): gdeng bskyed rtsal dbyung dbyings las rol pa'i gshen/ sgyu ma tsam du dbyings

20.1(1): che/ zur la tshom bu sgo dang sgo rgyan bcas/ lta ba'i khyung lding dur khrod gcan spyang 
20.2(1): rol/ de ltar bzhengs la bum pa lnga la sogs/ dbang gi sta gon chas rnams rdzogs 
20.3(1): par brgyan/ kun la nyi ma'i sa bon dang bcas pa/ 'phrul chen bzhi bcu rang 
20.4(1): bzhin med pa'i gsung / yi ge btu ba ci bzhin dgod par bya/ de nas rang lus 
20.5(1): rgyal ba'i dkyil 'khor la/ brten pa rtsa dang lus la don lngas ston/ dang po rlung lnga
